Task instruction sent to agent 
# Add New API Endpoint to Copilot Arena Server

**Repository:** copilot-arena-server (TheAgentCompany GitLab)  
**Difficulty:** MEDIUM  
**Category:** ccb_tac  
**Task Type:** API Development

## Description

Clone an API server codebase, understand the existing endpoint implementation patterns,
and add a new mock endpoint that mirrors an existing endpoint's response format.

**Why this benefits from MCP:**
- Understanding existing endpoint implementation patterns
- Finding how the `create_pair` endpoint works
- Understanding the API structure and return formats
- Navigating the codebase to find relevant files

## Task

1. Find copilot arena's API server codebase in GitLab 
   (http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/copilot-arena-server)
2. Clone the server repository to the /workspace folder
3. Start up the API server locally
4. Install the correct requirements by running `pip install -r requirements.txt`
5. Create a new POST endpoint to the server called `mock_create_pair`
6. It should return the same JSON as `create_pair`, except with "test" as both 
   the completions, rather than actually calling any APIs
7. Start the server in the background using:
   ```
   uvicorn app:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 5000 --workers 1 --log-config log_conf.yaml
   ```

## Success Criteria

[x] Repository cloned successfully  
[x] Server running on port 5000  
[x] mock_create_pair endpoint returns expected JSON format  
[x] Completions in response are "test" strings

## Notes

- This task tests understanding of existing API patterns
- MCP helps quickly understand the create_pair implementation
- Deterministic grading via API response validation

68-assistanttext-
Now I understand the response format. The `create_pair` endpoint returns a JSON with:
- `pairId`: a UUID string
- `completionItems`: array of 2 items, each with `completionId`, `userId`, `timestamp`, `completion`, `model`, etc.

The key fields for the mock endpoint are:
- The response should have the same structure
- The `completion` field should be "test" instead of actual API responses

Let me also check the test file to see what the expected response structure is.

     1→import yaml
     2→import base64
     3→import os
     4→from typing import List, Dict
     5→from dotenv import load_dotenv, find_dotenv
     6→
     7→
     8→def get_settings():
     9→    config_path = "config/app_config.yaml"
    10→    if os.path.exists(config_path):
    11→        with open(config_path, "r") as file:
    12→            return yaml.safe_load(file)
    13→
    14→    # Fall back to environment variable
    15→
    16→    load_dotenv(find_dotenv())
    17→    encoded_config = os.getenv("APP_CONFIG_YAML")
    18→    print("encoded config")
    19→    print(encoded_config)
    20→
    21→    # Decode base64 encoded YAML
    22→    try:
    23→        yaml_content = base64.b64decode(encoded_config).decode("utf-8")
    24→        return yaml.safe_load(yaml_content)
    25→    except Exception as e:
    26→        raise ValueError(f"Failed to decode configuration: {str(e)}")
    27→
    28→
    29→def get_models_by_tags(tags: List, models: List, tag_to_models: Dict):
    30→    if not tags or len(tags) == 0:
    31→        return models
    32→    tagged_models = set()
    33→    for tag in tags:
    34→        tagged_models.update(tag_to_models.get(tag, set()))
    35→    return list(tagged_models)
    36→
    37→
    38→def get_cost(prompt_token_length: int, response_token_length: int, model: str):
    39→    config = get_settings()
    40→    model_config = config["models"][model]
    41→    return (
    42→        prompt_token_length * model_config["input_cost"]
    43→        + response_token_length * model_config["output_cost"]
    44→    ) / 1000000
    45→

    33→            "authenticate": 0,
    34→            "create_user": 0,
    35→            "update_user": 0,
    36→            "delete_user": 0,
    37→        }
    38→
    39→    def track_function_call(self, function_name):
    40→        self.function_call_count[function_name] += 1
    41→        print(self.function_call_count)
    42→
    43→    def get_user_by_id(self, user_id: str):
    44→        self.track_function_call("get_user_by_id")
    45→        query = self.collection_ref.where(self.USER_ID_KEY, "==", user_id)
    46→        results = query.get()
    47→        if not results:
    48→            raise UserNotFoundError(f"User with ID {user_id} not found")
    49→        return results[0].to_dict()
    50→

Initialize empty DataFrame if fetch fails\n            self.global_outcomes_df = pd.DataFrame()\n\n    def add_client(self, client: IBaseClient):\n        for model in client.models:\n            if model in self.settings[\"models\"]:\n                self.model_clients[model] = client\n                for tag in self.settings[\"models\"][model][\"tags\"]:\n                    if tag not in self.tag_to_models:\n                        self.tag_to_models[tag] = set()\n                    self.tag_to_models[tag].add(model)\n\n        self.models = list(self.model_clients.keys())\n\n    def select_models(self, tags):\n        # Determine if this is an edit request\n        is_edit = \"edit\" in tags\n        dist_key = \"edit\" if is_edit else \"autocomplete\"\n\n        # Get available models with required tags\n        tagged_models = get_models_by_tags(tags, self.models, self.tag_to_models)\n        if len(tagged_models) == 0:\n            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f\"Error in tagged models\")\n\n        # Get all valid model pairs and their probabilities from the distribution\n        valid_pairs = []\n        probabilities = []\n\n        for pair_str, prob in self.distributions[dist_key].items():\n            model1, model2 = pair_str.split(\"|||\")\n            if model1 in tagged_models and model2 in tagged_models:\n                valid_pairs.append((model1, model2))\n                probabilities.append(prob)\n\n        if not valid_pairs:\n            raise HTTPException(\n                status_code=500, detail=f\"No valid model pairs found for tags: {tags}\"\n            )\n\n        # Normalize probabilities\n        total_prob = sum(probabilities)\n        if total_prob == 0:\n            raise HTTPException(\n                status_code=500, detail=\"Distribution probabilities sum to 0\"\n            )\n        normalized_probs = [p / total_prob for p in probabilities]\n\n        # Select a pair based on the normalized distribution\n        selected_pair = valid_pairs[\n            np.random.choice(len(valid_pairs), p=normalized_probs)\n        ]\n\n        # Randomly shuffle the order\n        if np.random.random() < 0.5:\n            selected_pair = selected_pair[::-1]\n\n        # Get the clients for the selected models\n        client1: IBaseClient = self.model_clients.get(selected_pair[0])\n        client2: IBaseClient = self.model_clients.get(selected_pair[1])\n\n        return list(selected_pair), client1, client2\n\n    def setup_routes(self):\n        @self.app.post(\"/create_edit_pair\")\n        @self.limiter.limit(\"300/minute\")\n        @handle_exceptions(self)\n        async def create_edit_pair(request: Request, background_tasks: BackgroundTasks):\n            start_time = time.time()\n            latency_breakdown = {}\n\n            # Decode the base64 string back to bytes\n        stored_hash = base64.b64decode(user[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY])\n        if not bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode(\"utf-8\"), stored_hash):\n            raise PasswordIncorrectError(\"Invalid username or password\")\n        return user\n\n    def create_user(\n        self, user_id: str, username: str, password: str, metadata: dict = None\n    ):\n        self.track_function_call(\"create_user\")\n        try:\n            self.get_user_by_username(username)\n            raise UsernameExistsError(\"Username already exists\")\n        except UserNotFoundError:\n            pass\n        user_data = {\n            self.USER_ID_KEY: user_id,\n            self.USERNAME_KEY: username,\n        }\n        if password is not None:\n            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode(\"utf-8\"), bcrypt.gensalt())\n            # Convert byte string to base64-encoded string\n            user_data[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY] = base64.b64encode(password_hash).decode(\n                \"utf-8\"\n            )\n        if metadata is not None:\n            user_data[self.METADATA_KEY] = metadata\n        self.collection_ref.add(user_data)\n\n    def update_user(\n        self,\n        username: str = None,\n        old_password: str = None,\n        new_password: str = None,\n        metadata: dict = None,\n    ):\n        self.track_function_call(\"update_user\")\n        user_doc = self.collection_ref.where(self.USERNAME_KEY, \"==\", username).get()\n        if not user_doc:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with username {username} not found\")\n        doc_id = user_doc[0].id\n        update_data = {}\n        self.authenticate(username, old_password)\n        if new_password:\n            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(\n                new_password.encode(\"utf-8\"), bcrypt.gensalt()\n            )\n            #     "content": "import base64\nfrom firebase_admin import firestore\nimport bcrypt\n\n\n# Custom Errors\nclass UserNotFoundError(Exception):\n    pass\n\n\nclass PasswordIncorrectError(Exception):\n    pass\n\n\nclass UsernameExistsError(Exception):\n    pass\n\n\nclass UserRepository:\n    # Constants for database keys\n    USER_ID_KEY = \"userId\"\n    USERNAME_KEY = \"username\"\n    PASSWORD_HASH_KEY = \"passwordHash\"\n    METADATA_KEY = \"metadata\"\n\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.db = firestore.client()\n        collection_name = \"users\"\n        self.collection_ref = self.db.collection(collection_name)\n        self.function_call_count = {\n            \"get_user_by_id\": 0,\n            \"get_user_by_username\": 0,\n            \"authenticate\": 0,\n            \"create_user\": 0,\n            \"update_user\": 0,\n            \"delete_user\": 0,\n        }\n\n    def track_function_call(self, function_name):\n        self.function_call_count[function_name] += 1\n        print(self.function_call_count)\n\n    def get_user_by_id(self, user_id: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"get_user_by_id\")\n        query = self.collection_ref.where(self.USER_ID_KEY, \"==\", user_id)\n        results = query.get()\n        if not results:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with ID {user_id} not found\")\n        return results[0].to_dict()\n\n    def get_user_by_username(self, username: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"get_user_by_username\")\n        query = self.collection_ref.where(self.USERNAME_KEY, \"==\", username)\n        results = query.get()\n        if not results:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with username {username} not found\")\n        return results[0].to_dict()\n\n    def authenticate(self, username: str, user_id: str, password: str = None):\n        self.track_function_call(\"authenticate\")\n        try:\n            user = self.get_user_by_id(user_id)\n        except:\n            user = self.get_user_by_username(username)\n\n        if self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY not in user.keys():\n            return user\n\n        if password is None:\n            raise PasswordIncorrectError(\"Invalid username or password\")\n\n        # Decode the base64 string back to bytes\n        stored_hash = base64.b64decode(user[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY])\n        if not bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode(\"utf-8\"), stored_hash):\n            raise PasswordIncorrectError(\"Invalid username or password\")\n        return user\n\n    def create_user(\n        self, user_id: str, username: str, password: str, metadata: dict = None\n    ):\n        self.track_function_call(\"create_user\")\n        try:\n            self.get_user_by_username(username)\n            raise UsernameExistsError(\"Username already exists\")\n        except UserNotFoundError:\n            pass\n        user_data = {\n            self.USER_ID_KEY: user_id,\n            self.USERNAME_KEY: username,\n        }\n        if password is not None:\n            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode(\"utf-8\"), bcrypt.gensalt())\n            # Convert byte string to base64-encoded string\n            user_data[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY] = base64.b64encode(password_hash).decode(\n                \"utf-8\"\n            )\n        if metadata is not None:\n            user_data[self.METADATA_KEY] = metadata\n        self.collection_ref.add(user_data)\n\n    def update_user(\n        self,\n        username: str = None,\n        old_password: str = None,\n        new_password: str = None,\n        metadata: dict = None,\n    ):\n        self.track_function_call(\"update_user\")\n        user_doc = self.collection_ref.where(self.USERNAME_KEY, \"==\", username).get()\n        if not user_doc:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with username {username} not found\")\n        doc_id = user_doc[0].id\n        update_data = {}\n        self.authenticate(username, old_password)\n        if new_password:\n            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(\n                new_password.encode(\"utf-8\"), bcrypt.gensalt()\n            )\n            # Convert byte string to base64-encoded string\n            update_data[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY] = base64.b64encode(\n                password_hash\n            ).decode(\"utf-8\")\n        if metadata:\n            update_data[self.METADATA_KEY] = metadata\n        self.collection_ref.document(doc_id).update(update_data)\n\n    def delete_user(self, user_id: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"delete_user\")\n        doc_ref = self.collection_ref.document(user_id)\n        if not doc_ref.get().exists:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with ID {user_id} not found\")\n        doc_ref.delete()\n",

  "originalFile": "import base64\nfrom firebase_admin import firestore\nimport firebase_admin\nimport bcrypt\n\n\n# Custom Errors\nclass UserNotFoundError(Exception):\n    pass\n\n\nclass PasswordIncorrectError(Exception):\n    pass\n\n\nclass UsernameExistsError(Exception):\n    pass\n\n\nclass UserRepository:\n    # Constants for database keys\n    USER_ID_KEY = \"userId\"\n    USERNAME_KEY = \"username\"\n    PASSWORD_HASH_KEY = \"passwordHash\"\n    METADATA_KEY = \"metadata\"\n\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.mock_mode = False\n        self.function_call_count = {\n            \"get_user_by_id\": 0,\n            \"get_user_by_username\": 0,\n            \"authenticate\": 0,\n            \"create_user\": 0,\n            \"update_user\": 0,\n            \"delete_user\": 0,\n        }\n        # Check if Firebase is initialized\n        try:\n            firebase_admin.get_app()\n            self.db = firestore.client()\n            collection_name = \"users\"\n            self.collection_ref = self.db.collection(collection_name)\n        except ValueError:\n            # Firebase not initialized, use mock mode\n            self.mock_mode = True\n            self.db = None\n            self.collection_ref = None\n            print(\"UserRepository running in mock mode - Firebase not initialized\")\n\n    def track_function_call(self, function_name):\n        self.function_call_count[function_name] += 1\n        print(self.function_call_count)\n\n    def get_user_by_id(self, user_id: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"get_user_by_id\")\n        if self.mock_mode:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with ID {user_id} not found (mock mode)\")\n        query = self.collection_ref.where(self.USER_ID_KEY, \"==\", user_id)\n        results = query.get()\n        if not results:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with ID {user_id} not found\")\n        return results[0].to_dict()\n\n    def get_user_by_username(self, username: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"get_user_by_username\")\n        query = self.collection_ref.where(self.USERNAME_KEY, \"==\", username)\n        results = query.get()\n        if not results:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with username {username} not found\")\n        return results[0].to_dict()\n\n    def authenticate(self, username: str, user_id: str, password: str = None):\n        self.track_function_call(\"authenticate\")\n        try:\n            user = self.get_user_by_id(user_id)\n        except:\n            user = self.get_user_by_username(username)\n\n        if self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY not in user.keys():\n            return user\n\n        if password is None:\n            raise PasswordIncorrectError(\"Invalid username or password\")\n\n        # Decode the base64 string back to bytes\n        stored_hash = base64.b64decode(user[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY])\n        if not bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode(\"utf-8\"), stored_hash):\n            raise PasswordIncorrectError(\"Invalid username or password\")\n        return user\n\n    def create_user(\n        self, user_id: str, username: str, password: str, metadata: dict = None\n    ):\n        self.track_function_call(\"create_user\")\n        try:\n            self.get_user_by_username(username)\n            raise UsernameExistsError(\"Username already exists\")\n        except UserNotFoundError:\n            pass\n        user_data = {\n            self.USER_ID_KEY: user_id,\n            self.USERNAME_KEY: username,\n        }\n        if password is not None:\n            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode(\"utf-8\"), bcrypt.gensalt())\n            # Convert byte string to base64-encoded string\n            user_data[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY] = base64.b64encode(password_hash).decode(\n                \"utf-8\"\n            )\n        if metadata is not None:\n            user_data[self.METADATA_KEY] = metadata\n        self.collection_ref.add(user_data)\n\n    def update_user(\n        self,\n        username: str = None,\n        old_password: str = None,\n        new_password: str = None,\n        metadata: dict = None,\n    ):\n        self.track_function_call(\"update_user\")\n        user_doc = self.collection_ref.where(self.USERNAME_KEY, \"==\", username).get()\n        if not user_doc:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with username {username} not found\")\n        doc_id = user_doc[0].id\n        update_data = {}\n        self.authenticate(username, old_password)\n        if new_password:\n            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(\n                new_password.encode(\"utf-8\"), bcrypt.gensalt()\n            )\n            # Convert byte string to base64-encoded string\n            update_data[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY] = base64.b64encode(\n                password_hash\n            ).decode(\"utf-8\")\n        if metadata:\n            update_data[self.METADATA_KEY] = metadata\n        self.collection_ref.document(doc_id).update(update_data)\n\n    def delete_user(self, user_id: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"delete_user\")\n        doc_ref = self.collection_ref.document(user_id)\n        if not doc_ref.get().exists:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with ID {user_id} not found\")\n        doc_ref.delete()\n",

Constants for database keys\n    USER_ID_KEY = \"userId\"\n    USERNAME_KEY = \"username\"\n    PASSWORD_HASH_KEY = \"passwordHash\"\n    METADATA_KEY = \"metadata\"\n\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.mock_mode = False\n        self.function_call_count = {\n            \"get_user_by_id\": 0,\n            \"get_user_by_username\": 0,\n            \"authenticate\": 0,\n            \"create_user\": 0,\n            \"update_user\": 0,\n            \"delete_user\": 0,\n        }\n        # Firebase not initialized, use mock mode\n            self.mock_mode = True\n            self.db = None\n            self.collection_ref = None\n            print(\"UserRepository running in mock mode - Firebase not initialized\")\n\n    def track_function_call(self, function_name):\n        self.function_call_count[function_name] += 1\n        print(self.function_call_count)\n\n    def get_user_by_id(self, user_id: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"get_user_by_id\")\n        if self.mock_mode:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with ID {user_id} not found (mock mode)\")\n        query = self.collection_ref.where(self.USER_ID_KEY, \"==\", user_id)\n        results = query.get()\n        if not results:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with ID {user_id} not found\")\n        return results[0].to_dict()\n\n    def get_user_by_username(self, username: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"get_user_by_username\")\n        if self.mock_mode:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with username {username} not found (mock mode)\")\n        query = self.collection_ref.where(self.USERNAME_KEY, \"==\", username)\n        results = query.get()\n        if not results:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with username {username} not found\")\n        return results[0].to_dict()\n\n    def authenticate(self, username: str, user_id: str, password: str = None):\n        self.track_function_call(\"authenticate\")\n        try:\n            user = self.get_user_by_id(user_id)\n        except:\n            user = self.get_user_by_username(username)\n\n        if self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY not in user.keys():\n            return user\n\n        if password is None:\n            raise PasswordIncorrectError(\"Invalid username or password\")\n\n        # Decode the base64 string back to bytes\n        stored_hash = base64.b64decode(user[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY])\n        if not bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode(\"utf-8\"), stored_hash):\n            raise PasswordIncorrectError(\"Invalid username or password\")\n        return user\n\n    def create_user(\n        self, user_id: str, username: str, password: str, metadata: dict = None\n    ):\n        self.track_function_call(\"create_user\")\n        if self.mock_mode:\n            print(f\"Mock create_user: {username}\")\n            return\n        try:\n            self.get_user_by_username(username)\n            raise UsernameExistsError(\"Username already exists\")\n        except UserNotFoundError:\n            pass\n        user_data = {\n            self.USER_ID_KEY: user_id,\n            self.USERNAME_KEY: username,\n        }\n        if password is not None:\n            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode(\"utf-8\"), bcrypt.gensalt())\n            # Convert byte string to base64-encoded string\n            user_data[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY] = base64.b64encode(password_hash).decode(\n                \"utf-8\"\n            )\n        if metadata is not None:\n            user_data[self.METADATA_KEY] = metadata\n        self.collection_ref.add(user_data)\n\n    def update_user(\n        self,\n        username: str = None,\n        old_password: str = None,\n        new_password: str = None,\n        metadata: dict = None,\n    ):\n        self.track_function_call(\"update_user\")\n        if self.mock_mode:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with username {username} not found (mock mode)\")\n        user_doc = self.collection_ref.where(self.USERNAME_KEY, \"==\", username).get()\n        if not user_doc:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with username {username} not found\")\n        doc_id = user_doc[0].id\n        update_data = {}\n        self.authenticate(username, old_password)\n        if new_password:\n            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(\n                new_password.encode(\"utf-8\"), bcrypt.gensalt()\n            )\n            # Convert byte string to base64-encoded string\n            update_data[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY] = base64.b64encode(\n                password_hash\n            ).decode(\"utf-8\")\n        if metadata:\n            update_data[self.METADATA_KEY] = metadata\n        self.collection_ref.document(doc_id).update(update_data)\n\n    def delete_user(self, user_id: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"delete_user\")\n        doc_ref = self.collection_ref.document(user_id)\n        if not doc_ref.get().exists:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with ID {user_id} not found\")\n        doc_ref.delete()\n",

        @self.app.post("/mock_create_pair")
        async def mock_create_pair(request: Request):
            """
            Mock endpoint that returns the same JSON structure as create_pair,
            but with "test" as both completions instead of calling actual APIs.
            """
            try:
                data = await request.json()
            except JSONDecodeError:
                error_msg = "Invalid JSON in request body"
                logger.info(error_msg)
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=error_msg)

            if "prefix" not in data or "userId" not in data or "privacy" not in data:
                error_msg = "Request must contain keys: [prefix, userId, privacy]"
                logger.info(error_msg)
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=error_msg)

            try:
                privacy = PrivacySetting(data.get("privacy"))
            except ValueError:
                raise HTTPException(
                    status_code=400,
                    detail=f"Invalid privacy value. Must be one of: {', '.join(PrivacySetting)}",
                )

6. EDIT /workspace/copilot-arena/server/src/firebase_client.py
Before
class FirebaseClient:
    def __init__(self):
        firebase_config_path = "config/firebase_config.json"
        if os.path.exists(firebase_config_path):
            self.cred = credentials.Certificate(firebase_config_path)
        else:
            load_dotenv(find_dotenv())
            encoded_key = os.getenv("FIREBASE_ACCOUNT_KEY")
            config_dict = json.loads(base64.b64decode(encoded_key).decode("utf-8"))
            self.cred = credentials.Certificate(config_dict)
        firebase_admin.initialize_app(self.cred)
        self.db = firestore.client()

class FirebaseClient:
    def __init__(self):
        self.mock_mode = False
        firebase_config_path = "config/firebase_config.json"
        if os.path.exists(firebase_config_path):
            self.cred = credentials.Certificate(firebase_config_path)
        else:
            load_dotenv(find_dotenv())
            encoded_key = os.getenv("FIREBASE_ACCOUNT_KEY")
            if not encoded_key:
                # Enable mock mode when no Firebase credentials are available
                self.mock_mode = True
                self.cred = None
                self.db = None
                self.call_timestamps = {}
                self.function_call_count = {
                    "upload_data": 0,
                    "get_autocomplete_outcomes": 0,
                    "get_autocomplete_outcomes_count": 0,
                }
                print("FirebaseClient running in mock mode - no credentials available")
                return
            config_dict = json.loads(base64.b64decode(encoded_key).decode("utf-8"))
            self.cred = credentials.Certificate(config_dict)
        firebase_admin.initialize_app(self.cred)
        self.db = firestore.client()
        self.call_timestamps = {}
        self.function_call_count = {
            "upload_data": 0,
            "get_autocomplete_outcomes": 0,
            "get_autocomplete_outcomes_count": 0,
        }

import base64
import os
from firebase_admin import firestore
import firebase_admin
import bcrypt


# Custom Errors
class UserNotFoundError(Exception):
    pass


class PasswordIncorrectError(Exception):
    pass


class UsernameExistsError(Exception):
    pass


class UserRepository:
    # Constants for database keys
    USER_ID_KEY = "userId"
    USERNAME_KEY = "username"
    PASSWORD_HASH_KEY = "passwordHash"
    METADATA_KEY = "metadata"

    def __init__(self):
        self.mock_mode = False
        self.function_call_count = {
            "get_user_by_id": 0,
            "get_user_by_username": 0,
            "authenticate": 0,
            "create_user": 0,
            "update_user": 0,
            "delete_user": 0,
        }
        # Check if Firebase is initialized
        try:
            firebase_admin.get_app()
            self.db = firestore.client()
            collection_name = "users"
            self.collection_ref = self.db.collection(collection_name)
        except ValueError:
            # Firebase not initialized, use mock mode
            self.mock_mode = True
            self.db = None
            self.collection_ref = None
            print("UserRepository running in mock mode - Firebase not initialized")

14. EDIT /workspace/copilot-arena/server/src/user_repository.py
Before
    def create_user(
        self, user_id: str, username: str, password: str, metadata: dict = None
    ):
        self.track_function_call("create_user")
        try:
            self.get_user_by_username(username)
            raise UsernameExistsError("Username already exists")
        except UserNotFoundError:
            pass
        user_data = {
            self.USER_ID_KEY: user_id,
            self.USERNAME_KEY: username,
        }
        if password is not None:
            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode("utf-8"), bcrypt.gensalt())
            # Convert byte string to base64-encoded string
            user_data[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY] = base64.b64encode(password_hash).decode(
                "utf-8"
            )
        if metadata is not None:
            user_data[self.METADATA_KEY] = metadata
        self.collection_ref.add(user_data)
After
    def create_user(
        self, user_id: str, username: str, password: str, metadata: dict = None
    ):
        self.track_function_call("create_user")
        if self.mock_mode:
            print(f"Mock create_user: {username}")
            return
        try:
            self.get_user_by_username(username)
            raise UsernameExistsError("Username already exists")
        except UserNotFoundError:
            pass
        user_data = {
            self.USER_ID_KEY: user_id,
            self.USERNAME_KEY: username,
        }
        if password is not None:
            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode("utf-8"), bcrypt.gensalt())
            # Convert byte string to base64-encoded string
            user_data[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY] = base64.b64encode(password_hash).decode(
                "utf-8"
            )
        if metadata is not None:
            user_data[self.METADATA_KEY] = metadata
        self.collection_ref.add(user_data)

class GCPClient:
    def __init__(
        self,
        project_id: str = "code-arena",
        credentials_path: str = "config/firebase_config.json",
    ):
        """
        Initialize GCP client with project and credentials.

        Args:
            project_id: The Google Cloud project ID
            credentials_path: Path to the service account credentials JSON file
        """
        self.mock_mode = False
        import os
        if not os.path.exists(credentials_path):
            self.mock_mode = True
            self.storage_client = None
            logger.info("GCPClient running in mock mode - no credentials available")
            return
        self.storage_client = storage.Client.from_service_account_json(
            credentials_path, project=project_id
        )
